separator="true">,</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></msub></mfrac><mroot><mrow><mn>3</mn><mi>k</mi><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><msubsup><mi>r</mi><mrow><mi>s</mi><mo displaystyle="true"><mi>x</mi></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>p</mi></msub><mo>+</mo><mroot><mrow><mn>3</mn><mi>k</mi><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><msubsup><mi>r</mi><mrow><mi>s</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><mn>3</mn></msubsup></mrow><mn>3</mn></mroot><mfrac><mrow><msub><mi>x</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>p</mi></msub></mrow><msub><mi>r</mi><mrow><mi>s</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></msub></mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex"> \begin{align*} \frac{dx}{dt} &amp;= k \frac{x - x_p}{\left((x - x_p) \frac{r_{s,0}}{x_0 - x_p}\right)^3} \\ &amp;= k \frac{x - x_p}{(x - x_p)^3 \frac{r_{s,0}^3}{(x_0 - x_p)^3}} \\ &amp;= k \frac{(x_0 - x_p)^3}{(x - x_p)^2 r_{s,0}^3}, \\ \frac{dt}{dx} &amp;= \frac{r_{s,0}^3}{k(x_0 - x_p)^3} (x - x_p)^2, \\ \int_0^t dt &amp;= \frac{r_{s,0}^3}{k(x_0 - x_p)^3} \int_{x_0}^x (x - x_p)^2 dx, \\ t &amp;= \frac{r_{s,0}^3}{k(x_0 - x_p)^3} \left[\frac{1}{3} (x - x_p)^3\right]_{x_0}^x \\ &amp;= \frac{r_{s,0}^3}{3k(x_0 - x_p)^3} \left((x - x_p)^3 - (x_0 - x_p)^3\right) \\ &amp;= \frac{r_{s,0}^3}{3k(x_0 - x_p)^3} (x - x_p)^3 - \frac{r_{s,0}^3}{3k}, \\ \frac{r_{s,0}^3}{3k(x_0 - x_p)^3} (x - x_p)^3 &amp;= t + \frac{r_{s,0}^3}{3k}, \\ (x - x_p)^3 &amp;= \frac{3k(x_0 - x_p)^3}{r_{s,0}^3}t + (x_0 - x_p)^3, \\ x - x_p &amp;= \frac{x_0 - x_p}{r_{s,0}} \sqrt[3]{3kt + r_{s,0}^3}, \\ x &amp;= x_p + \sqrt[3]{3kt + r_{s,0}^3} \frac{x_0 - x_p}{r_{s,0}}. \end{align*} </annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html"
